Check-in: Although it was a holiday, the check-in went smoothly and there was not a long wait.
Room: I booked a twin room with a bathtub. The room was spacious and comfortable, and more business-style.
Hotel facilities: If you order takeout, there is a table for takeout at the front desk of the hotel (no delivery robot). The hotel has a swimming pool, which I didn't experience this time.
Breakfast: I arrived at the restaurant at 8:30 and found a seat smoothly. The food was standard and not particularly rich. It was enough to fill you up. There were freshly cooked wontons, noodles, rice noodles, etc.
Surrounding environment: There is a water sports center within 500m, with cruise ships and kayaks to play, 100 yuan per hour; there is also an open-air children's playground and a dog-walking playground in Xinye Square. The children had a lot of fun playing karts and trampolines.
Overall, I was very satisfied with the stay. After checking out, I received a call from the hotel saying that I had left a power bank behind. The staff took the initiative to ask for the address and sent it to the courier.
